### Eastern Europe ###

	## St. Petersburg ##

		petrograd_renaming_act = {
			picture = petrograd_city
			potential = {
				primary_culture = russian
				NOT = { has_country_flag = peters_city_renamed }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = names_of_the_revolution }
				owns = 994
				any_greater_power = {
					war_with = THIS
					is_culture_group = germanic
				}
			}

			allow = {
				mass_politics = 1
			}

			effect = {
				set_country_flag = peters_city_renamed
				994 = {
					change_province_name = "Petrograd"
					state_scope = { change_region_name = "Petrograd Oblast" }
				}
				war_exhaustion = -5
				any_pop = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					dominant_issue = { factor = 0.1 value = jingoism }
					militancy = -1
				}
			}

			ai_will_do = {
				factor = 1
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					NOT = { war_exhaustion = 20 }
				}
			}
		}

		petrograd_renaming_act2 = {
			picture = petrograd_city
			potential = {
				is_culture_group = germanic
				994 = {
					owner = {
						primary_culture = russian
						has_country_flag = peters_city_renamed
						NOT = { has_country_flag = names_of_the_revolution }
						vassal_of = THIS
					}
				}
			}
			allow = {
				mass_politics = 1
			}

			effect = {
				clr_country_flag = peters_city_renamed
				994 = {
					change_province_name = "St. Peterburg"
					state_scope = { change_region_name = "St. Peterburg" }
				}
				prestige = 20
				any_pop = {
					limit = { is_primary_culture = yes }
					dominant_issue = { factor = 0.1 value = jingoism }
					militancy = -1
				}
			}

			ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		}

								}
								change_province_name = "Møgeltønder"
								clr_global_flag = german_renamed_3333
							}
						}
					}

				## German ##

					random_owned = {
						limit = { owner = { is_culture_group = germanic } }
						owner = {
							random_owned = {
								limit = {
									province_id = 370
									NOT = { has_global_flag = german_renamed_370 }
								}
								change_province_name = "Flensburg"
								state_scope = { change_region_name = "Schleswig" }
								set_global_flag = german_renamed_370
							}
							random_owned = {
								limit = {
									province_id = 371
									NOT = { has_global_flag = german_renamed_371 }
								}
								change_province_name = "Apenrade"
								set_global_flag = german_renamed_371
							}
							random_owned = {
								limit = {
									province_id = 3333
									NOT = { has_global_flag = german_renamed_3333 }
								}
								change_province_name = "Mögeltondern"
								set_global_flag = german_renamed_3333
							}
						}
					}
			}

			ai_will_do = { factor = 1 }
		}

		# Sjaelland
		rename_DEN_372 = {
			picture = gtfo
			potential = {
				DEN_372 = { owned_by = THIS }
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_culture_group = scandinavian
						OR = {
							AND = { owns = 372 has_global_flag = german_renamed_372 }
							AND = { owns = 373 has_global_flag = german_renamed_373 }
						}
					}
					AND = {
						is_culture_group = germanic
						OR = {
							AND = { owns = 372 NOT = { has_global_flag = german_renamed_372 } }
							AND = { owns = 373 NOT = { has_global_flag = german_renamed_373 } }
						}
					}
				}
			}

			allow = {
				war = no
				state_n_government = 1
			}
